COMMUNICATIONS\n12.1\n\nIntroduction\n\n- Communications includes\n\ntelemetry downlinks, command up-\n\nlinks and radar tracking for the PDS and one or more attached payloads,\n\nThe\nseveral available communication links between payload, Shuttle, ground and satellites\nhave been analyzed in Section 1 . .\n22\nThe interfaces between Shuttle systems and\npayloads are defined and their
